Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 6:
Complex rational in t with P terms. Let me check if as t→∞, the t²/(c1+t²)→1 terms dominate. We get P·(c0+c4) + P^c5·(c8)·exp(c7·t). For finite t, the structure involves rational functions of t, not exp(-ct). Cannot exactly match P·exp(-ct).
Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 7:
`P*c0 + P*c1*log(c2*Abs(P)+1) + P*c3/(c4*Abs(P)+1) + P**c5*c6*exp(c7*t) + c8*t*exp(c9*t)`

Set c5=1/3, c7=0 → c6·P^(1/3). But then need P·exp(-ct). No such term available. The P terms are P, P·log(P), P/(aP+1). Can P·c0 + P·c1·log(c2|P|+1) + P·c3/(c4|P|+1) = P·exp(-ct)? No, these have no t-dependence. Set c8=0. Then only t-dependent term is P^c5·c6·exp(c7·t). One term can't match both P^(1/3) and P·exp(-ct).
Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 8-50: Let me continue checking key candidates.

### Candidate 14:
`P*c0 + P*c1 + P**c2*c3 + P**c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*t*exp(c8*t)`

Set c7=0, c2=1/3, c4=1, c6=-0.0858, c0+c1=0. → c3·P^(1/3) + c5·P·exp(c6·t). ✓
Candidate 14 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 22:
`P*P**c0*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3*exp(P*c4) + P**c5*c6*exp(c7*t) + c8*t*exp(c9*t)`

P·P^c0 = P^(c0+1). Set c0+1=1/3 → c0=-2/3. Set c2=0, c3=0 (or c4=0 making exp(Pc4)=1, absorbed). Set c5=1, c7=-0.0858, c8=0. Then c1·P^(1/3) + c6·P·exp(c7·t). Need c3=0 to kill exp(Pc4). ✓
Candidate 22 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 28:
`P*P**c0*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3*log(P*c4+1) + P**c5*c6*exp(c7*t) + c8*t*exp(c9*t)`

Set c0=-2/3 → P^(1/3)·c1. Set c2=0, c3=0, c5=1, c7=-0.0858, c8=0. ✓
Candidate 28 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 31:
`P*c0 + P**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4 + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*exp(c8*t)`

Set c1=1/3, c3=0 → c2·P^(1/3). Need P·exp(-ct). P*c0 is P·const, not P·exp. c5·exp, c7·exp have no P. Cannot produce P·exp(-ct).
Candidate 31 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 43:
`P*c0*sin(c1*t+c2) + P*c3 + P**c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)`

sin can't match exp(-ct) exactly.
Candidate 43 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 23:
`P**2*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P**c3*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*t*exp(c7*t)`

Set c0=0, c6=0, c3=1/3, c5=0 → c4·P^(1/3). Then P*c2 is static. Need P·exp(-ct). Not available.
Or set c3=1, c5=-0.0858 → c4·P·exp. Then need P^(1/3) from P²·exp or P·c2. Neither works.
Candidate 23 verdict: [NO MATCH]

Let me quickly scan remaining candidates for those with both P**c and P*exp(ct) terms:

### Candidate 48:
`P*c0 + P**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4 + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*exp(c8*t)*log(c9*Abs(P)+1)`

Set c1=1/3, c3=0 → P^(1/3). Need P·exp(-ct). P*c0 is static. c7·exp·log(P) ≠ P·exp. No.
Candidate 48 verdict: [NO MATCH]
